\"text\": \"The etcd MVCC compaction system involves multiple layers of abstraction and coordination between revision indices, watch streams, and slow watch detection.\\n\\n## Compaction Schedule\\n\\netcd implements two compaction strategies in the v3compactor package:\\n\\n1. **Periodic Compaction** (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go): The Periodic class implements time-based retention compaction. It maintains a sliding window of revisions, recording revisions at regular 1/10 intervals of the retention period and compacting the oldest revision every retention period.\\n\\n2. **Revision-based Compaction** (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go): The Revision class implements revision number-based retention. It runs every 5 minutes and compacts revisions older than (current_revision - retention_number).\\n\\n## Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nThe core compaction logic is in the MVCC storage layer:\\n\\n1. **Main Compaction Trigger** (server/storage/mvcc/kvstore.go): The Compact() function is the primary entry point that initiates compaction. It calls updateCompactRev() to validate and schedule the compaction revision, then delegates to compact() which schedules the actual work.\\n\\n2. **Compaction Execution** (server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go): The scheduleCompaction() function performs the actual compaction work in batches. It compacts the index using kvindex.Compact() to get the set of revisions to keep, then iterates through the database deleting key revisions that are not in the keep set.\\n\\n3. **Index Compaction** (server/storage/mvcc/index.go): The treeIndex.Compact() method removes outdated revisions from the index.\\n\\n4. **Key-level Compaction** (server/storage/mvcc/key_index.go): The compact() and doCompact() functions handle compaction at the individual key level, removing old generation histories and tombstones for revisions before the compaction point.\\n\\n## Watch Stream Cancellation on Compaction\\n\\nWatchers are notified when a compacted revision spans their observed history:\\n\\n1. **Watch Stream Initialization** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): When a watch is created with a startRev that is before the current compacted revision, or when a watcher's minRev falls behind the compactMainRev during operation, the watcher must be notified.\\n\\n2. **Compaction Notification Mechanism** (server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go): The chooseAll() function detects watchers with minRev < compactRev and sends them a WatchResponse containing the CompactRevision field instead of normal events. This is the key mechanism for canceling watches that span a compacted revision.\\n\\n3. **WatchResponse Structure** (server/storage/mvcc/watcher.go): The WatchResponse struct includes a CompactRevision field (line 97) which is set when a watcher is cancelled due to compaction. When clients receive a response with CompactRevision set, they know their watch has been interrupted and must restart from a later revision.\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nThe system detects and manages slow watchers through a \\\"victim\\\" mechanism:\\n\\n1. **Slow Watcher Classification** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): When a watcher is created with a startRev older than currentRev, it is classified as \\\"unsynced\\\" (line 148-149). The slowWatcherGauge metric tracks the count of these unsynced slow watchers (line 411).\\n\\n2. **Watcher Batching and Victims** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): The syncWatchers() function processes unsynced watchers in batches. When a watcher's channel becomes full and cannot accept events (line 390-391), the watcher is marked as a \\\"victim\\\" and moved to a separate victims list for retry.\\n\\n3. **Victim Processing Loop** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): The syncVictimsLoop() and moveVictims() functions attempt to retry sending events to victim watchers with 10ms retry intervals. Slow watchers that block event sending are tracked and reported via the slowWatcherGauge metric.\\n\\n4. **Metrics and Monitoring** (server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go): The slowWatcherGauge tracks the total number of unsynced slow watchers, providing visibility into how many clients are lagging behind the latest revisions.\\n\\n## Coordination\\n\\nThe entire compaction system is coordinated through:\\n- Revision locks (revMu) protecting currentRev and compactMainRev\\n- Batch transactional operations for atomic database updates\\n- Scheduled job queue (fifoSched) for sequential compaction execution\\n- Watch group synchronization during the compaction process to ensure watchers are notified before their historical data is deleted\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":252,"cache_read_input_tokens":51609,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":252},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"afbd7ab3-44d5-450c-8a00-e83f90a6935f","uuid":"95dbf2f1-c845-448b-a095-2c0a58f8477b"}

\"text\": \"The etcd MVCC compaction system involves multiple layers of abstraction and coordination between revision indices, watch streams, and slow watch detection.\\n\\n## Compaction Schedule\\n\\netcd implements two compaction strategies in the v3compactor package:\\n\\n1. **Periodic Compaction** (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go): The Periodic class implements time-based retention compaction. It maintains a sliding window of revisions, recording revisions at regular 1/10 intervals of the retention period and compacting the oldest revision every retention period.\\n\\n2. **Revision-based Compaction** (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go): The Revision class implements revision number-based retention. It runs every 5 minutes and compacts revisions older than (current_revision - retention_number).\\n\\n## Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nThe core compaction logic is in the MVCC storage layer:\\n\\n1. **Main Compaction Trigger** (server/storage/mvcc/kvstore.go): The Compact() function is the primary entry point that initiates compaction. It calls updateCompactRev() to validate and schedule the compaction revision, then delegates to compact() which schedules the actual work.\\n\\n2. **Compaction Execution** (server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go): The scheduleCompaction() function performs the actual compaction work in batches. It compacts the index using kvindex.Compact() to get the set of revisions to keep, then iterates through the database deleting key revisions that are not in the keep set.\\n\\n3. **Index Compaction** (server/storage/mvcc/index.go): The treeIndex.Compact() method removes outdated revisions from the index.\\n\\n4. **Key-level Compaction** (server/storage/mvcc/key_index.go): The compact() and doCompact() functions handle compaction at the individual key level, removing old generation histories and tombstones for revisions before the compaction point.\\n\\n## Watch Stream Cancellation on Compaction\\n\\nWatchers are notified when a compacted revision spans their observed history:\\n\\n1. **Watch Stream Initialization** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): When a watch is created with a startRev that is before the current compacted revision, or when a watcher's minRev falls behind the compactMainRev during operation, the watcher must be notified.\\n\\n2. **Compaction Notification Mechanism** (server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go): The chooseAll() function detects watchers with minRev < compactRev and sends them a WatchResponse containing the CompactRevision field instead of normal events. This is the key mechanism for canceling watches that span a compacted revision.\\n\\n3. **WatchResponse Structure** (server/storage/mvcc/watcher.go): The WatchResponse struct includes a CompactRevision field (line 97) which is set when a watcher is cancelled due to compaction. When clients receive a response with CompactRevision set, they know their watch has been interrupted and must restart from a later revision.\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nThe system detects and manages slow watchers through a \\\"victim\\\" mechanism:\\n\\n1. **Slow Watcher Classification** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): When a watcher is created with a startRev older than currentRev, it is classified as \\\"unsynced\\\" (line 148-149). The slowWatcherGauge metric tracks the count of these unsynced slow watchers (line 411).\\n\\n2. **Watcher Batching and Victims** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): The syncWatchers() function processes unsynced watchers in batches. When a watcher's channel becomes full and cannot accept events (line 390-391), the watcher is marked as a \\\"victim\\\" and moved to a separate victims list for retry.\\n\\n3. **Victim Processing Loop** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): The syncVictimsLoop() and moveVictims() functions attempt to retry sending events to victim watchers with 10ms retry intervals. Slow watchers that block event sending are tracked and reported via the slowWatcherGauge metric.\\n\\n4. **Metrics and Monitoring** (server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go): The slowWatcherGauge tracks the total number of unsynced slow watchers, providing visibility into how many clients are lagging behind the latest revisions.\\n\\n## Coordination\\n\\nThe entire compaction system is coordinated through:\\n- Revision locks (revMu) protecting currentRev and compactMainRev\\n- Batch transactional operations for atomic database updates\\n- Scheduled job queue (fifoSched) for sequential compaction execution\\n- Watch group synchronization during the compaction process to ensure watchers are notified before their historical data is deleted\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Schedule\\n\\netcd implements two compaction strategies in the v3compactor package:\\n\\n1. **Periodic Compaction** (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go): The Periodic class implements time-based retention compaction. It maintains a sliding window of revisions, recording revisions at regular 1/10 intervals of the retention period and compacting the oldest revision every retention period.\\n\\n2. **Revision-based Compaction** (server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go): The Revision class implements revision number-based retention. It runs every 5 minutes and compacts revisions older than (current_revision - retention_number).\\n\\n## Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nThe core compaction logic is in the MVCC storage layer:\\n\\n1. **Main Compaction Trigger** (server/storage/mvcc/kvstore.go): The Compact() function is the primary entry point that initiates compaction. It calls updateCompactRev() to validate and schedule the compaction revision, then delegates to compact() which schedules the actual work.\\n\\n2. **Compaction Execution** (server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go): The scheduleCompaction() function performs the actual compaction work in batches. It compacts the index using kvindex.Compact() to get the set of revisions to keep, then iterates through the database deleting key revisions that are not in the keep set.\\n\\n3. **Index Compaction** (server/storage/mvcc/index.go): The treeIndex.Compact() method removes outdated revisions from the index.\\n\\n4. **Key-level Compaction** (server/storage/mvcc/key_index.go): The compact() and doCompact() functions handle compaction at the individual key level, removing old generation histories and tombstones for revisions before the compaction point.\\n\\n## Watch Stream Cancellation on Compaction\\n\\nWatchers are notified when a compacted revision spans their observed history:\\n\\n1. **Watch Stream Initialization** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): When a watch is created with a startRev that is before the current compacted revision, or when a watcher's minRev falls behind the compactMainRev during operation, the watcher must be notified.\\n\\n2. **Compaction Notification Mechanism** (server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go): The chooseAll() function detects watchers with minRev < compactRev and sends them a WatchResponse containing the CompactRevision field instead of normal events. This is the key mechanism for canceling watches that span a compacted revision.\\n\\n3. **WatchResponse Structure** (server/storage/mvcc/watcher.go): The WatchResponse struct includes a CompactRevision field (line 97) which is set when a watcher is cancelled due to compaction. When clients receive a response with CompactRevision set, they know their watch has been interrupted and must restart from a later revision.\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nThe system detects and manages slow watchers through a \\\"victim\\\" mechanism:\\n\\n1. **Slow Watcher Classification** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): When a watcher is created with a startRev older than currentRev, it is classified as \\\"unsynced\\\" (line 148-149). The slowWatcherGauge metric tracks the count of these unsynced slow watchers (line 411).\\n\\n2. **Watcher Batching and Victims** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): The syncWatchers() function processes unsynced watchers in batches. When a watcher's channel becomes full and cannot accept events (line 390-391), the watcher is marked as a \\\"victim\\\" and moved to a separate victims list for retry.\\n\\n3. **Victim Processing Loop** (server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go): The syncVictimsLoop() and moveVictims() functions attempt to retry sending events to victim watchers with 10ms retry intervals. Slow watchers that block event sending are tracked and reported via the slowWatcherGauge metric.\\n\\n4. **Metrics and Monitoring** (server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go): The slowWatcherGauge tracks the total number of unsynced slow watchers, providing visibility into how many clients are lagging behind the latest revisions.\\n\\n## Coordination\\n\\nThe entire compaction system is coordinated through:\\n- Revision locks (revMu) protecting currentRev and compactMainRev\\n- Batch transactional operations for atomic database updates\\n- Scheduled job queue (fifoSched) for sequential compaction execution\\n- Watch group synchronization during the compaction process to ensure watchers are notified before their historical data is
